# Compares if the CURRENT (neighbor or opposing scope) is techs AHEAD of the prior, likely ROOT scope
POP_GetTechCost = {
	export_to_key = { lhs = $return$ value = modifier:$type$_tech_cost_modifier }
}
POP_GetTechCostTotal = {
	export_to_key = { lhs = $return$ value = modifier:technology_cost }
}
POP_GetTechCostInstitutions = {
	#export_to_key = { lhs = $return$ value = total_tech_penalty } ### DOESNT WORK ###THEN WHY ISN'T IT COMMENTED OUT
}
POP_GetTechDiff = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			tech_difference = 25
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tech_difference = 38
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					tech_difference = 44
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						tech_difference = 47
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							tech_difference = 49
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								tech_difference = 50
							}
							set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 50 }
						}
						else = {
							set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 49 }
						}
					}
					else = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								tech_difference = 48
							}
							set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 48 }
						}
						else = {
							set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 47 }
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							tech_difference = 45

			}
			else = {

				else = {

						else = {

					else = {

			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						tech_difference = 28

							limit = {
								tech_difference = 5
							}
							set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 5 }

						else = {
							set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 4 }
						}
					}
					else = {
						set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 3 }

				}
				else = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							tech_difference = 1
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								tech_difference = 2
							}
							set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 2 }

							set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 1 }
						}
					}

						set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 0 }
					}
				}
			}

	}
}

POP_GetAdminEffic = {
	export_to_key = { lhs = $return$ value = modifier:administrative_efficiency }
	change_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 1 }
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			adm_tech = 59
		}
		change_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 0.05 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			adm_tech = 57
		}
		change_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 0.05 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			adm_tech = 55
		}
		change_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 0.05 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			adm_tech = 51
		}

	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			adm_tech = 47
		}

	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			adm_tech = 45
		}
		change_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 0.05 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			adm_tech = 42
		}
		change_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 0.05 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			adm_tech = 39
		}

	}
	if = {

}

POP_GetMerchant = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			num_of_merchants = 16
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				num_of_merchants = 24
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					num_of_merchants = 28
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						num_of_merchants = 30
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							num_of_merchants = 31
						}
						set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 31 }
					}
					else = {
						set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 30 }
					}
				}
				else = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							num_of_merchants = 29
						}
						set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 29 }
					}
					else = {
						set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 28 }
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						num_of_merchants = 26
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							num_of_merchants = 27
						}
						set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 27 }

							num_of_merchants = 25

				num_of_merchants = 8

						set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 12 }

						}

						set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 2 }

						}
						set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 1 }
					}
					else = {
						set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 0 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

POP_GetMerc = {
	set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 0 }
	trigger_switch = {
		on_trigger = num_of_mercenaries
		128 = {
			trigger_switch = {
				on_trigger = num_of_mercenaries
				192 = {
					trigger_switch = {
						on_trigger = num_of_mercenaries

							trigger_switch = {

														}

POP_AddKeepHighest = {
    remove_building = keep_$type$_0
    remove_building = keep_$type$_1
    remove_building = keep_$type$_2
    remove_building = keep_$type$_3
    remove_building = keep_$type$_4
    remove_building = keep_$type$_5
    remove_building = keep_$type$_6

    if = {
        limit = {
            can_build = keep_$type$_6
        }
        add_building = keep_$type$_6
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            can_build = keep_$type$_5
        }
        add_building = keep_$type$_5
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            can_build = keep_$type$_4
        }
        add_building = keep_$type$_4
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            can_build = keep_$type$_3
        }
        add_building = keep_$type$_3
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            can_build = keep_$type$_2
        }
        add_building = keep_$type$_2
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            can_build = keep_$type$_1
        }
        add_building = keep_$type$_1
    }
}

POP_GetMaint = {
	export_to_key = {
		lhs = $return$
		value = trigger_value:$type$_maintenance
	}
}
POP_GetFacInf = {
	set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 0 }
	if = { limit = { faction_influence = { faction = FC_$FAC$ influence = 50 } }
		if = { limit = { faction_influence = { faction = FC_$FAC$ influence = 75 } }
			if = { limit = { faction_influence = { faction = FC_$FAC$ influence = 88 } }
				if = { limit = { faction_influence = { faction = FC_$FAC$ influence = 94 } }
					if = { limit = { faction_influence = { faction = FC_$FAC$ influence = 97 } }
						if = { limit = { faction_influence = { faction = FC_$FAC$ influence = 99 } }
							if = { limit = { faction_influence = { faction = FC_$FAC$ influence = 100 } }
								set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 100 }
							}
							else = {
								set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 99 }
							}
						}
						else = {
							if = { limit = { faction_influence = { faction = FC_$FAC$ influence = 98 } }
								set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 98 }
							}
							else = {
								set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 97 }
							}
						}
					}
					else = {
						if = { limit = { faction_influence = { faction = FC_$FAC$ influence = 95 } }
							if = { limit = { faction_influence = { faction = FC_$FAC$ influence = 96 } }
								set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 96 }
							}
							else = {
								set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 95 }
							}
						}
						else = {
							set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 94 }
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					if = { limit = { faction_influence = { faction = FC_$FAC$ influence = 91 } }

								set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 83 }

POP_GetOutputHelper = {
    if = {
        limit = {
            has_province_flag = Prod_S$slot$
            check_key = { lhs = Prod_S$slot$ value = $from$ }

            NOT = {
                check_key = { lhs = Prod_S$slot$ value = $to$ }
            }
        }
        change_key = { lhs = $return$ which = Prod_S$slot$IncomeProd }
    }
}

POP_GetTlrncHelper = {
    if = {
        limit = {
            $religion$ = 1
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                $religion$ = 1.5
            }
            set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 1.5 }
        }
        else = {
            set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 1 }
        }
    }
    else = {
        if = {
            limit = {
                $religion$ = 0.5
            }
            set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 0.5 }
        }
        else = {
            set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 0 }
        }
    }
}

POP_GetTlrnc = {
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_key = { lhs = $var$ value = 37 }
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                check_key = { lhs = $var$ value = 53 }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    check_key = { lhs = $var$ value = 60 }
                }
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        check_key = { lhs = $var$ value = 62 }
                    }
                    if = {
                        limit = {
                            check_key = { lhs = $var$ value = 63 }
                        }
                        if = {
                            limit = {
                                check_key = { lhs = $var$ value = 66 }
                            }
                            POP_GetTlrncHelper = { religion = polynesian_religion return = $return$ }
                        }
                        else = {

POP_CalcLandTime = {
    set_key = { lhs = Land_Travel value = 1.8 } # base difficulty for CE, core balancer
	[[Innate]
    multiply_key = { lhs = Land_Travel value = $Innate$ }
	]
	[[Forest]
    set_key = { lhs = CE_Tmp0 value = $Forest$ } # role of woods/trees
    multiply_key = { lhs = CE_Tmp0 which = Modi_CEForest }
    change_key = { lhs = CE_Tmp0 value = 1 }
    multiply_key = { lhs = Land_Travel which = CE_Tmp0 }
	]
	[[Height]
    set_key = { lhs = CE_Tmp0 value = $Height$ } # role of woods/trees
    multiply_key = { lhs = CE_Tmp0 which = Modi_CEHeight }
    change_key = { lhs = CE_Tmp0 value = 1 }
    multiply_key = { lhs = Land_Travel which = CE_Tmp0 }
	]
	[[Desert]
    set_key = { lhs = CE_Tmp0 value = $Desert$ } # role of woods/trees
    multiply_key = { lhs = CE_Tmp0 which = Modi_CEDesert }
    change_key = { lhs = CE_Tmp0 value = 1 }
    multiply_key = { lhs = Land_Travel which = CE_Tmp0 }
	]
    multiply_key = { lhs = Land_Travel which = Modi_CE }
    set_key = { lhs = CE_Tmp0 value = 0 }
}

POP_GetLandTime = { 
    trigger_switch = {
        on_trigger = has_terrain
        
        arctic = {
			POP_CalcLandTime = { Innate=5 }
        }
        forest_flats = {
			POP_CalcLandTime = { Forest=1 }
        }
        forest_hills = {
			POP_CalcLandTime = { Height=0.5 Forest=1 }
        }
        forest_mountains = {
			POP_CalcLandTime = { Height=1.75 Forest=1 }
        }
        forest_highlands = {
			POP_CalcLandTime = { Height=1 Forest=1 }
        }
        wood_flats = {
			POP_CalcLandTime = { Forest=0.5 }
        }
        wood_hills = {
			POP_CalcLandTime = { Height=0.5 Forest=0.5 }
        }
        wood_mountains = {
			POP_CalcLandTime = { Height=1.75 Forest=0.5 }
        }
        wood_highlands = {
			POP_CalcLandTime = { Height=1 Forest=0.5 }
        }
        shrub_flats = {
			POP_CalcLandTime = { Forest=0.15 }
        }
        shrub_hills = {
			POP_CalcLandTime = { Height=0.5 Forest=0.15 }
        }
        shrub_mountains = {
			POP_CalcLandTime = { Height=1.75 Forest=0.15 }
        }
        shrub_highlands = {
			POP_CalcLandTime = { Height=1 Forest=0.15 }
        }
        grass_flats = {
			POP_CalcLandTime = yes
        }
        grass_hills = {
			POP_CalcLandTime = { Height=0.5 }
        }
        grass_mountains = {
			POP_CalcLandTime = { Height=1.75 }
        }
        grass_highlands = {
			POP_CalcLandTime = { Height=1 }
        }
        desert_flats = {
			POP_CalcLandTime = { Desert=1.5 }
        }
        desert_hills = {
			POP_CalcLandTime = { Height=0.5 Desert=1.5 }
        }
        desert_mountains = {
			POP_CalcLandTime = { Height=1.75 Desert=1.5 }
        }
        desert_highlands = {
			POP_CalcLandTime = { Height=1 Desert=1.5 }
        }
        jungle_flats = {
			POP_CalcLandTime = { Forest=2 }
        }
        jungle_hills = {
			POP_CalcLandTime = { Height=0.5 Forest=2 }
        }
        floodplains = {
			POP_CalcLandTime = { Innate=2 }
        }
        taiga = {
			POP_CalcLandTime = { Forest=3 }
        }
        marsh = {
			POP_CalcLandTime = { Innate=2.5 }
        }
        tundra = {
			POP_CalcLandTime = { Innate=1.5 Forest=1.5 }
        }
        alpine_tundra = {
			POP_CalcLandTime = { Height=1.75 }
        }
        small_island = {
			POP_CalcLandTime = yes
        }
    }
}

													}

														on_trigger = devastation
														22 = { set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 22 } }
														21 = { set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 21 } }
													}
												}
											}
										}
										18 = {

												on_trigger = devastation
												20 = { set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 20 } }
												19 = { set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 19 } }
												18 = { set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 18 } }
											}
										}
									}
								}
								12 = {
									trigger_switch = {
										on_trigger = devastation
										15 = {
											trigger_switch = {
												on_trigger = devastation
												17 = { set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 17 } }
												16 = { set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 16 } }
												15 = { set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 15 } }
											}
										}
										12 = {
											trigger_switch = {
												on_trigger = devastation
												14 = { set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 14 } }
												13 = { set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 13 } }
												12 = { set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 12 } }
											}
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
						1 = {
							trigger_switch = {
								on_trigger = devastation
								6 = {
									trigger_switch = {
										on_trigger = devastation
										9 = {
											trigger_switch = {
												on_trigger = devastation
												11 = { set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 11 } }
												10 = { set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 10 } }
												9 = { set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 9 } }
											}
										}
										6 = {
											trigger_switch = {
												on_trigger = devastation

												7 = { set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 7 } }
												6 = { set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 6 } }
											}
										}
									}
								}
								1 = {
									trigger_switch = {

												2 = { set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 2 } }

POP_SetDevastationHelper = {
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_key = { lhs = Public_Tmp1 value = $val$ }
        }
        subtract_key = { lhs = Public_Tmp1 value = $val$ }

        add_devastation = $val$
    }
}

POP_SetDevastation = {
    set_key = { lhs = Public_Tmp1 $type$ = $inp$ }

    POP_SetDevastationHelper = { val = 64 }
    POP_SetDevastationHelper = { val = 32 }
    POP_SetDevastationHelper = { val = 16 }
    POP_SetDevastationHelper = { val = 8 }
    POP_SetDevastationHelper = { val = 4 }
    POP_SetDevastationHelper = { val = 2 }
    POP_SetDevastationHelper = { val = 1 }
    POP_SetDevastationHelper = { val = 0.5 }
    POP_SetDevastationHelper = { val = 0.25 }
    POP_SetDevastationHelper = { val = 0.1 }

    set_key = { lhs = Public_Tmp1 value = 0 }
}

POP_GetDucatHelper = {
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_key = { lhs = Tmp_Misc0 value = $val$ }
        }
        subtract_key = { lhs = Tmp_Misc0 value = $val$ }

        add_treasury = $val$
    }
}

POP_GetDucat = {
    set_key = { lhs = Tmp_Misc0 $type$ = $inp$ }
    while = {
        limit = {
            check_key = { lhs = Tmp_Misc0 value = 32768 }
        }
        subtract_key = { lhs = Tmp_Misc0 value = 32768 }

        add_treasury = 32768
    }
    POP_GetDucatHelper = { val = 16384 }
    POP_GetDucatHelper = { val = 8192 }
    POP_GetDucatHelper = { val = 4096 }
    POP_GetDucatHelper = { val = 2048 }
    POP_GetDucatHelper = { val = 1024 }
    POP_GetDucatHelper = { val = 512 }
    POP_GetDucatHelper = { val = 256 }
    POP_GetDucatHelper = { val = 128 }
    POP_GetDucatHelper = { val = 64 }
    POP_GetDucatHelper = { val = 32 }
    POP_GetDucatHelper = { val = 16 }
    POP_GetDucatHelper = { val = 8 }
    POP_GetDucatHelper = { val = 4 }
    POP_GetDucatHelper = { val = 2 }
    POP_GetDucatHelper = { val = 1 }

    set_key = { lhs = Tmp_Misc0 value = 0 }
}

POP_RemoveDucatHelper = {
    if = {
        limit = {
            check_key = { lhs = POP_RemoveDucatInp value = $val$ }
        }
        subtract_key = { lhs = POP_RemoveDucatInp value = $val$ }

        add_treasury = -$val$
    }
}

POP_RemoveDucat = {
    set_key = { lhs = POP_RemoveDucatInp $type$ = $inp$ }
    while = {
        limit = {
            check_key = { lhs = POP_RemoveDucatInp value = 32768 }
        }
        subtract_key = { lhs = POP_RemoveDucatInp value = 32768 }

        add_treasury = -32768
    }
    POP_RemoveDucatHelper = { val = 16384 }
    POP_RemoveDucatHelper = { val = 8192 }
    POP_RemoveDucatHelper = { val = 4096 }
    POP_RemoveDucatHelper = { val = 2048 }
    POP_RemoveDucatHelper = { val = 1024 }
    POP_RemoveDucatHelper = { val = 512 }
    POP_RemoveDucatHelper = { val = 256 }
    POP_RemoveDucatHelper = { val = 128 }
    POP_RemoveDucatHelper = { val = 64 }
    POP_RemoveDucatHelper = { val = 32 }
    POP_RemoveDucatHelper = { val = 16 }
    POP_RemoveDucatHelper = { val = 8 }
    POP_RemoveDucatHelper = { val = 4 }
    POP_RemoveDucatHelper = { val = 2 }
    POP_RemoveDucatHelper = { val = 1 }

    set_key = { lhs = POP_RemoveDucatInp value = 0 }
}

POP_SumWealth = {
    set_key = { lhs = Class_Wealth value = 0 }

    change_key = { lhs = Class_Wealth which = SF_Wealth }
    change_key = { lhs = Class_Wealth which = NM_Wealth }
    change_key = { lhs = Class_Wealth which = RE_Wealth }
    change_key = { lhs = Class_Wealth which = NO_Wealth }
    change_key = { lhs = Class_Wealth which = BG_Wealth }
    change_key = { lhs = Class_Wealth which = CL_Wealth }
	change_key = { lhs = Class_Wealth which = Infra_Wealth }
}

clear_income_modifier = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_$type$_modifier = $modname$_$value$ 
		}
		remove_$type$_modifier = $modname$_$value$
	}
}

POP_ClassTotalCalc = {
    set_key = { lhs = Class_Rural which = SF_Total }
    change_key = { lhs = Class_Rural which = NM_Total }

    set_key = { lhs = Class_Urban which = RE_Total }

    set_key = { lhs = Class_Notables which = NO_Total }
    change_key = { lhs = Class_Notables which = BG_Total }
    change_key = { lhs = Class_Notables which = CL_Total }

    set_key = { lhs = Class_Total which = Class_Rural }
    change_key = { lhs = Class_Total which = Class_Urban }
    change_key = { lhs = Class_Total which = Class_Notables }
}

POP_SetClass = {
    if = { limit = { NOT = { check_key = { lhs = SF_Total value = 0 } } } set_key = { lhs = SF_Total value = 0 } }
    if = { limit = { NOT = { check_key = { lhs = NM_Total value = 0 } } } set_key = { lhs = NM_Total value = 0 } }
    if = { limit = { NOT = { check_key = { lhs = RE_Total value = 0 } } } set_key = { lhs = RE_Total value = 0 } }
    if = { limit = { NOT = { check_key = { lhs = NO_Total value = 0 } } } set_key = { lhs = NO_Total value = 0 } }
    if = { limit = { NOT = { check_key = { lhs = BG_Total value = 0 } } } set_key = { lhs = BG_Total value = 0 } }
    if = { limit = { NOT = { check_key = { lhs = CL_Total value = 0 } } } set_key = { lhs = CL_Total value = 0 } }
    
	POP_ClassTotalCalc = yes
	
    set_key = { lhs = SF_Ratio which = SF_Total }
	divide_key = { lhs = SF_Ratio which = Class_Total }
	multiply_key = { lhs = SF_Ratio value = 100 }
    set_key = { lhs = NM_Ratio which = NM_Total }
	divide_key = { lhs = NM_Ratio which = Class_Total }
	multiply_key = { lhs = NM_Ratio value = 100 }
	
	set_key = { lhs = RE_Ratio which = RE_Total }
	divide_key = { lhs = RE_Ratio which = Class_Total }
	multiply_key = { lhs = RE_Ratio value = 100 }
	
	set_key = { lhs = NO_Ratio which = NO_Total }
	divide_key = { lhs = NO_Ratio which = Class_Total }
	multiply_key = { lhs = NO_Ratio value = 100 }
	set_key = { lhs = BG_Ratio which = BG_Total }
	divide_key = { lhs = BG_Ratio which = Class_Total }
	multiply_key = { lhs = BG_Ratio value = 100 }
	set_key = { lhs = CL_Ratio which = CL_Total }
	divide_key = { lhs = CL_Ratio which = Class_Total }
	multiply_key = { lhs = CL_Ratio value = 100 }
	
	set_key = { lhs = Class_RuralR which = Class_Rural }
	divide_key = { lhs = Class_RuralR which = Class_Total }
	multiply_key = { lhs = Class_RuralR value = 100 }
	set_key = { lhs = Class_UrbanR which = Class_Urban }
	divide_key = { lhs = Class_UrbanR which = Class_Total }
	multiply_key = { lhs = Class_UrbanR value = 100 }
	set_key = { lhs = Class_NotablesR which = Class_Notables }
	divide_key = { lhs = Class_NotablesR which = Class_Total }
	multiply_key = { lhs = Class_NotablesR value = 100 }
	
	MN_GetSlot_Class = yes
	MN_Recompute = { type = RurP }
	MN_Recompute = { type = UrbP }
	MN_Recompute = { type = NotP }
}


# Returns a random number between 0 and 0.999
POP_GetRandomNumber = {
    set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 0 }

    random_list = {
        1 = {
        }
        1 = {
            change_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 0.001 }
        }
        1 = {
            change_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 0.002 }
        }
        1 = {
            change_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 0.003 }
        }
        1 = {
            change_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 0.004 }
        }
        1 = {
            change_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 0.005 }
        }
        1 = {
            change_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 0.006 }
        }
        1 = {
            change_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 0.007 }
        }
        1 = {
            change_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 0.008 }
        }
        1 = {
            change_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 0.009 }
        }
    }

    random_list = {
        1 = {
        }
        1 = {
            change_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 0.01 }
        }
        1 = {
            change_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 0.02 }
        }
        1 = {
            change_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 0.03 }
        }
        1 = {
            change_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 0.04 }
        }
        1 = {
            change_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 0.05 }
        }
        1 = {
            change_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 0.06 }
        }
        1 = {
            change_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 0.07 }

        1 = {
            change_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 0.08 }
        }
        1 = {
            change_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 0.09 }
        }
    }

    random_list = {
        1 = {
        }
        1 = {
            change_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 0.1 }
        }
        1 = {
            change_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 0.2 }
        }
        1 = {

        1 = {

        }
        1 = {
            change_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 0.9 }
        }
    }

# Get a random number from a range between from and to
POP_GetRandomRange = {
    set_key = { lhs = POP_GetRandomRangeMult value = $to$ }
    subtract_key = { lhs = POP_GetRandomRangeMult value = $from$ }

    POP_GetRandomNumber = {
        return = $return$
    }

    multiply_key = { lhs = $return$ which = POP_GetRandomRangeMult }
    change_key = { lhs = $return$ value = $from$ }

    set_key = { lhs = POP_GetRandomRangeMult value = 0 }
}

# It is fired on normal province and returns as event target its corresponding tradenode center
POP_GetTradenode = {
    tradenode_centers = {
        limit = {
            is_key_equal = { lhs = ID_TN which = PREV }
        }
        save_event_target_as = $return$
    }
}

# Input parameters:
# Coord_X, Coord_Y = coordinate variables name
# targ1, targ2 = scopes to calculate distance between
# return = name of the variable where the finished value is stored
# What it does:
# It calculates distance between two scopes who has x and y coordinate variables
POP_GetDist = {
    $targ1$ = {
        set_key = { lhs = Xdiff which = $Coord_X$ }
        set_key = { lhs = Ydiff which = $Coord_Y$ }

        $targ2$ = {
            set_key = { lhs = Xdiff which = $Coord_X$ }
            set_key = { lhs = Ydiff which = $Coord_Y$ }

            PREV = {
                subtract_key = { lhs = Xdiff which = PREV }
                subtract_key = { lhs = Ydiff which = PREV }
            }

            set_key = { lhs = Xdiff value = 0 }
            set_key = { lhs = Ydiff value = 0 }
        }

        if = {
            limit = {
                NOT = { check_key = { lhs = Xdiff value = 0 } }
            }
            multiply_key = { lhs = Xdiff value = -1 }
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                NOT = { check_key = { lhs = Ydiff value = 0 } }
            }
            multiply_key = { lhs = Ydiff value = -1 }
        }

        # Distance approximation without sqrt given abs X and Y diff between 2 points
        set_key = { lhs = XYsum value = 0.001 }
        change_key = { lhs = XYsum which = Xdiff }
        change_key = { lhs = XYsum which = Ydiff }

        set_key = { lhs = XYmult which = Xdiff }
        multiply_key = { lhs = XYmult which = Ydiff }
        multiply_key = { lhs = XYmult value = 1.135 }

        if = { # same effect as what game does, but without the report in the error log
            limit = {
                is_key_equal = { lhs = XYsum value = 0 }
            }
            set_key = { lhs = XYsum value = 0.001 }
        }

        divide_key = { lhs = XYmult which = XYsum }
        subtract_key = { lhs = XYsum which = XYmult }

        PREV = {
            set_key = { lhs = XYsum which = PREV }

            set_key = { lhs = $return$ which = XYsum }

            set_key = { lhs = XYsum value = 0 }
        }

        set_key = { lhs = XYsum value = 0 }
        set_key = { lhs = XYmult value = 0 }
        set_key = { lhs = Xdiff value = 0 }
        set_key = { lhs = Ydiff value = 0 }
    }
}

# Input:
# varname = name of the variable binary modifier is being based on
# value = view an example below
# type = country or province
# modname = name of the binary modifier being set
# It is a script used to maintain a set of binary modifiers
# Example:
#    set_variable = {
#        which = some_var
#        value = 11.56
#    }
#
#    POP_SetMod = {
#        varname = some_var
#        modname = some_mod
#        type = province
#        value = 8
#    }
#    POP_SetMod = {
#        varname = some_var
#        modname = some_mod
#        type = province
#        value = 4
#    }
#    POP_SetMod = {
#        varname = some_var
#        modname = some_mod
#        type = province
#        value = 2
#    }
#    POP_SetMod = {
#        varname = some_var
#        modname = some_mod
#        type = province
#        value = 1
#    }
POP_SetMod = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_key = { lhs = $varname$ value = $value$ }
		}
		subtract_key = { lhs = $varname$ value = $value$ }
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { 
                    has_$type$_modifier = $modname$_$value$ 
                }
			}
			add_$type$_modifier = {
				name = $modname$_$value$	 
				duration = -1
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_$type$_modifier = $modname$_$value$
		}
		remove_$type$_modifier = $modname$_$value$
	}
}
POP_AddMod = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_key = { lhs = $varname$ value = $value$ }
		}
		subtract_key = { lhs = $varname$ value = $value$ }
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { 
                    has_$type$_modifier = $modname$_$value$ 
                }
			}
			add_$type$_modifier = {
				name = $modname$_$value$	 
				duration = -1
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
	}
}
POP_ClrMod = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_$type$_modifier = $modname$_$value$
		}
		remove_$type$_modifier = $modname$_$value$
	}
}

init_as_zero = {
	change_key = { lhs = $variable$ value = 0 }
}
POP_GetHordeUnity = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			horde_unity = 53.125
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				horde_unity = 78.125
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					horde_unity = 90.625
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						horde_unity = 96.875
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							horde_unity = 100.0
						}
						set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 100.0 }
					}
					else = {
						set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 96.875 }
					}
				}
				else = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							horde_unity = 93.75
						}
						set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 93.75 }
					}
					else = {
						set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 90.625 }
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						horde_unity = 84.375
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							horde_unity = 87.5
						}
						set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 87.5 }
					}
					else = {
						set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 84.375 }
					}
				}
				else = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							horde_unity = 81.25
						}
						set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 81.25 }
					}
					else = {
						set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 78.125 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					horde_unity = 65.625
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						horde_unity = 71.875
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							horde_unity = 75.0
						}
						set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 75.0 }
					}
					else = {
						set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 71.875 }
					}
				}
				else = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							horde_unity = 68.75
						}
						set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 68.75 }
					}
					else = {
						set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 65.625 }
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						horde_unity = 59.375
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							horde_unity = 62.5
						}
						set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 62.5 }
					}
					else = {
						set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 59.375 }
					}
				}
				else = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							horde_unity = 56.25
						}
						set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 56.25 }
					}
					else = {
						set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 53.125 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				horde_unity = 28.125
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					horde_unity = 40.625
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						horde_unity = 46.875
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							horde_unity = 50.0
						}
						set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 50.0 }
					}
					else = {
						set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 46.875 }
					}
				}
				else = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							horde_unity = 43.75
						}
						set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 43.75 }
					}
					else = {
						set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 40.625 }
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						horde_unity = 34.375
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							horde_unity = 37.5
						}
						set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 37.5 }
					}
					else = {
						set_key = { lhs = $return$ value = 34.375 }
					}
				}
				else = {
					if = {
